# SAP Completes Acquisition of SmartRecruiters, Delivering Innovation and AI-Powered Recruiting Differentiation for Global Enterprises

September 11, 2025 10:07 ET | Source: SmartRecruiters Follow SmartRecruiters

---

Share

---

SAN FRANCISCO, Sept. 11, 2025 (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- SAP SE (NYSE: SAP) today announced it has completed the acquisition of SmartRecruiters, the Recruiting AI Company. Together, SAP and SmartRecruiters will accelerate innovation in talent acquisition while giving customers confidence, flexibility, scale, and the only platform built to meet the full spectrum of enterprise hiring needs, helping organizations attract, engage, and hire top talent.

Innovation at Speed

With SAP’s global scale and SmartRecruiters’ category-defining platform, customers can expect faster delivery of AI-powered capabilities, end-to-end orchestrated talent solutions, and user experiences that directly support business outcomes. The combined roadmap will accelerate innovation across candidate engagement, recruiter efficiency, and hiring manager experience.

One-of-a-Kind Differentiation

SmartRecruiters is uniquely positioned to serve the dual needs of the modern enterprise: high-volume, frontline hiring and enterprise-grade corporate recruiting. Built from the ground up as an AI-native platform, SmartRecruiters delivers flexibility, scale, and measurable impact. Together with SAP, SmartRecruiters sets a new standard for how enterprises compete for talent in today’s dynamic market.

Customer Stability and Focus

SmartRecruiters will continue to serve customers in two ways:

- For SAP SuccessFactors customers: SmartRecruiters’ modern recruiting innovation will be integrated into the SuccessFactors suite, enhancing the platform with AI-enabled capabilities that improve time-to-hire, elevate candidate and hiring manager experiences, and deliver deeper analytics for workforce planning.
- For SmartRecruiters customers: SmartRecruiters will continue to operate as a standalone recruiting solution, fully interoperable with SuccessFactors and other HCM systems, supported by the same team, same focus on innovative capabilities, and the same integrations they rely on today.

Why it Matters

“Hiring the right people has never been more critical to business success,” said Rebecca Carr, CEO of SmartRecruiters. “By joining SAP, we will accelerate our pace of innovation while giving customers the confidence they need and the flexibility they demand. SmartRecruiters’ unique one-two punch, high-volume hiring plus corporate recruiting, built on an AI-native foundation, makes us the only platform designed for the full spectrum of enterprise hiring challenges.”

"The SAP acquisition of SmartRecruiters sends a clear message: talent acquisition is not just operational, but central to enterprise transformation in the age of AI," said Claudia Birle, head of Global Talent Acquisition at Continental, AG. "By combining SAP’s global scale with SmartRecruiters’ innovative, AI-powered platform, organizations like Continental will be better equipped to hire smarter and drive business growth."

See for Yourself

This fall, SmartRecruiters, an SAP Company, will be live at the industry’s most influential events. Our team will share the roadmap, demonstrate AI-powered capabilities already delivering results, and give you a firsthand look at what’s next.

It’s your chance to sit down directly with the leaders behind SmartRecruiters, ask questions, see the product in action, and explore how our platform can help you hire at speed and scale.

- HR Tech, Las Vegas – September 16–18
- SuccessConnect, Las Vegas – October 6–8

- Gartner ReimagineHR US, Orlando – October 27–29

More than 140 million candidates, and 4,000 organizations, including Amazon, Visa, and McDonald’s, rely on SmartRecruiters to build winning teams.

[SAP to Acquire SmartRecruiters: Integrating Innovative Talent Acquisition Portfolio Will Help Customers Attract and Retain Top Talent] SAP to Acquire SmartRecruiters: Integrating Innovative Talent Acquisition Portfolio Will Help Customers Attract and Retain Top Talent Accessibility Statement Skip Navigation

WALLDORF, Germany and SAN FRANCISCO, Aug. 1, 2025 /PRNewswire/ -- SAP (NYSE: SAP) and SmartRecruiters today announced that SAP has entered into an agreement to acquire SmartRecruiters, a leading talent acquisition (TA) software provider. SmartRecruiters' deep expertise in high-volume recruiting, recruitment automation, and AI-enabled candidate experience and engagement are considered an ideal addition to the SAP SuccessFactors human capital management (HCM) suite. The planned acquisition will strengthen SAP's all-in-one HCM suite, so customers have the tools they need to attract and retain top talent in an increasingly competitive landscape.

SmartRecruiters' powerful, user-friendly interfaces and seamless workflows will complement SAP's robust HR tools – improving decision-making, reducing time-to-hire and providing a better experience for candidates. Embedded analytics and AI-driven recommendations from both companies will provide rich insights into talent pools, hiring bottlenecks and workforce planning.

"Hiring the right people is not just an HR priority – it's a business priority. With this planned acquisition, we will help our customers attract and hire the best talent so they can advance their talent acquisition agendas with speed and agility, while lowering their total cost of ownership," said Muhammad Alam, member of the Executive Board of SAP SE, SAP Product & Engineering. "Customers will be able to manage the entire candidate lifecycle — from sourcing and interviewing to onboarding and beyond — all in a single system to streamline the experience for recruiters, hiring managers, and, in particular, candidates."

Customers can expect enhanced and AI-enabled recruiting and hiring capabilities, making applicant tracking and candidate screening more efficient. Data-driven hiring and recruitment analytics will flow directly into SAP's existing HCM tools, providing a single system of record and harmonized data for compliant, seamless operations. The SmartRecruiters portfolio will also continue to be available standalone for the foreseeable future.

SmartRecruiters' Software-as-a-Service solutions and platform enable more than 4,000 organizations globally to efficiently manage their hiring workflows end-to-end, offering a compelling experience to recruiters, hiring managers and candidates.

SmartRecruiters CEO, Rebecca Carr said, "SmartRecruiters' mission has always been to make hiring easy. Joining forces with SAP presents a tremendous opportunity for enterprises worldwide to benefit from our industry leading approach to talent acquisition. I couldn't be more excited for the opportunity this planned acquisition presents for our customers, partners and employees as we build the future of hiring together."

Best Enterprise LMS Software: 20 Perfect Options 

 

 

 

 

Reports show that the LMS market is expected to grow by almost 250% by 2033, and that’s for a reason. Around 91% of L&D pros say human skills are increasingly important for business growth. And LMSs for enterprises are perceived as the best way to upskill employees.

Businesses often start with their own learning solution, but as the company grows, something bigger, more powerful, and more efficient is needed. In this article, we’ve chosen the 20 best enterprise LMS software options that offer more than simple employee training and can cover most big business needs. Let’s examine them together!

## What is an enterprise LMS, and how should you choose one?

Choosing an LMS is easy when you need to gather your 15 employees together and show them the working rules. Basically, PowerPoint and any screencasting app are a good fit. But as the company grows, it gets harder to train dozens or hundreds or thousands of people.

One day, you’ll need a solution that enables you to author your own courses, make them interactive, and track results — and before you know it, the list of requirements gets extremely long! At that point, you’re looking for a bigger solution: probably an AI-powered, enterprise-level LMS that supports all your HR processes and organizational needs.

So, finding the best enterprise LMS that will cover all big enterprises’ ambitions and needs is not a simple task. For those seeking a quick solution to this challenge, we prepared a comparison chart of the best enterprise LMSs. For more details, click on the LMS or scroll down.

| Enterprise LMS systems | Scalability | Integrations | Extended-enterprise* | Authoring and content | Mobile-friendly |

| iSpring LMS | Top enterprise LMS scalability | Albato, RESTful API, SSO, HRIS, CRMs and more | From authoring to selling | Strong (via iSpring Suite) | Native mobile app |
| Cornerstone Learning | Highly scalable | HRIS, SSO, APIs | Strong | Moderate | Native mobile app |
| Docebo | Top enterprise LMS scalability | API ecosystem | Excellent | Built-in tools | Mobile App publisher |
| 360Learning | Strong | SSO, HRIS | Moderate | Very strong | Native mobile app |

**--- Result 3 ---**

```
[SAP SuccessFactors Pricing Tiers & Costs] (https://peoplemanagingpeople.com/tools/sap-successfactors-pricing/)
SAP SuccessFactors Pricing Tiers & Costs

Skip to main content

SAP SuccessFactors is a human capital management (HCM) software that offers multiple products, pricing tiers, and plans, typically on a subscription basis.

HR professionals use SAP SuccessFactors to manage various HR functions, including talent management, payroll, and workforce planning.

This guide covers everything you need to know about SAP SuccessFactors plans and pricing to help you make an informed purchase decision with confidence.

## How Much Does SAP SuccessFactors Cost?

There are multiple products to choose from within the SuccessFactors suite, so the total cost of SAP SuccessFactors will depend on which you decide to purchase.

Certain modules, like the SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting, are priced per transaction, which includes any messages, jobs, actions, responses, or tasks processed via the cloud service​.

## SAP SuccessFactors Plans & Pricing Tiers

Here's an overview of the available SAP SuccessFactors plans:

| Plan Type | Price | What’s Included? |
| --- | --- | --- |
| SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central | $8 per user per month or annual subscription beginning at $85 per employee | Core HR, Payroll, Time Tracking, Benefits Admin, Document Management, Digital Workplace, Employee Central Service Center, Employee Central Payroll |
| SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting | $180.00/transaction/year | Global Talent Sourcing, Applicant Management, Onboarding Portal, Performance Management, Compensation Management, Learning Management, Succession Planning |
| SAP SuccessFactors Workforce Analytics | $3,770.00 | Advanced Reporting and Analytics, Predictive Insights, Data Integration, Interactive Dashboards, Benchmarking, Metrics on Workforce Performance |

SAP SucessFactors pricing plans overview. Contact SAP directly for a more precise estimate.

Let’s break down the available SAP SuccessFactors plans a bit further:

### SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central

Ideal for mid-sized companies, this plan focuses on core HR functions such as payroll, time tracking, and benefits administration.

It is suited for organizations looking to streamline HR processes and improve employee management.

Core features include a flexible HRIS and centralized document management.

Limitations include a lack of advanced talent management features.

## What is SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central?

SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central is a cloud-based HRIS designed to streamline global HR processes and provide real-time insights for informed HR decisions.

Get the Cloud HCM Buyer's Guide and find out what your peers are saying about SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central, Workday, SAP SuccessFactors and more!

SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central is the #15 ranked solution in top Cloud HCM solutions. PeerSpot users give SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central an average rating of 8.4 out of 10. SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central is most commonly compared to Workday: SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central vs Workday.

## Featured SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central reviews

Senior Consultant

There are some activities that we perform in SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central and similar activities that we must also perform in Employee Central Payroll. If information has been entered in Employee Central, why is there a need to add the same information in another module of SAP SuccessFactors? This duplication of activities is a concern we have faced. One thing is opened in SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central, and the same activity must be performed in Employee Central Payroll as well. If the product is the same and contains two to three modules, why does SAP require us to perform duplication of work under the same product? The pricing is very high. There is significant competition in the market, and we face challenges in selling the product due to the high prices that SAP is offering. SAP needs to reconsider their pricing strategy.

Read full review

SP

Senior ERP Consultant at a manufacturing company with 10,001+ employees

SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central is cloud-based, eliminating the need for any infrastructure with readily available data centers. It is very user-friendly and integrates seamlessly with the Employee Central Payroll and all other talent modules. I have utilized the payroll integration, noting that on-premises payroll is called SAP

## Comparison Buyer's Guide

Download the report

Executive SummaryUpdated on Feb 22, 2026

SAP SuccessFactors and SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central compete within the HR software market. SAP SuccessFactors appears to have a broader functionality, while Employee Central is superior in core HR tasks for streamlined management.

Features: SAP SuccessFactors includes modules for talent management, performance analysis, and learning management. Employee Central features core HR functions, global payroll management, and self-service options.

Ease of Deployment and Customer Service: SAP SuccessFactors offers flexible deployment and strong customer support. Employee Central provides rapid deployment with ongoing support, focusing on user-friendly implementation for HR needs.

Pricing and ROI: SAP SuccessFactors involves a higher initial cost for its comprehensive features, offering long-term ROI. Employee Central requires a lower initial investment, leading to quicker ROI for core HR functions due to cost-efficiency.

DOWNLOAD THE COMPLETE REPORT

## 3 Answers

Last answered Feb 5, 2026

Senior Consultant

Consultant

Top 10

Feb 5, 2026

There are some activities that we perform in SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central and similar activities that we must also perform in Employee Central Payroll. If information has been entered in Employee Central, why is there a need to add the same information in another module of SAP SuccessFactors? This duplication of activities is a concern we have faced. One thing is opened in SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central, and the same activity must be performed in Employee Central Payroll as well. If the product is the same and contains two to three modules, why does SAP require us to perform duplication of work under the same product? The pricing is very high. There is significant competition in the market, and we face challenges in selling the product due to the high prices that SAP is offering. SAP needs to reconsider their pricing strategy.

Like(0)

Reply

## What is SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central?

SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central is a cloud-based HRIS designed to streamline global HR processes and provide real-time insights for informed HR decisions.

Get the Cloud HCM Buyer's Guide and find out what your peers are saying about SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central, Workday, SAP SuccessFactors and more!

SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central is the #15 ranked solution in top Cloud HCM solutions. PeerSpot users give SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central an average rating of 8.4 out of 10. ## Featured SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central reviews

Senior Consultant

There are some activities that we perform in SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central and similar activities that we must also perform in Employee Central Payroll. If information has been entered in Employee Central, why is there a need to add the same information in another module of SAP SuccessFactors? This duplication of activities is a concern we have faced. One thing is opened in SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central, and the same activity must be performed in Employee Central Payroll as well. If the product is the same and contains two to three modules, why does SAP require us to perform duplication of work under the same product? The pricing is very high. There is significant competition in the market, and we face challenges in selling the product due to the high prices that SAP is offering. SAP needs to reconsider their pricing strategy.

## Comparison Buyer's Guide

Download the report

Executive SummaryUpdated on Feb 22, 2026

SAP SuccessFactors and SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central compete within the HR software market. SAP SuccessFactors appears to have a broader functionality, while Employee Central is superior in core HR tasks for streamlined management.

Features: SAP SuccessFactors includes modules for talent management, performance analysis, and learning management. Employee Central features core HR functions, global payroll management, and self-service options.

Ease of Deployment and Customer Service: SAP SuccessFactors offers flexible deployment and strong customer support. Employee Central provides rapid deployment with ongoing support, focusing on user-friendly implementation for HR needs.

Pricing and ROI: SAP SuccessFactors involves a higher initial cost for its comprehensive features, offering long-term ROI. Employee Central requires a lower initial investment, leading to quicker ROI for core HR functions due to cost-efficiency.

DOWNLOAD THE COMPLETE REPORT

To learn more, read our detailed SAP SuccessFactors vs. SAP SuccessFactors Employee Central Report(Updated: March 2026).

After evaluating 14 HR platforms, Rippling is my top pick overall, BambooHR is the most ideal for small teams, Gusto is optimal for new businesses, and ADP Workforce Now is the best fit for midsize firms.

## How does HR software improve your business processes?

Human resources (HR) software systems unify administration, recruitment, payroll, training, employee engagement, performance management, and other essential HR functions.

This provides a secure database of employee data and a centralized view of the company. It also helps HR teams effectively manage each stage of the employee life cycle.

The right HR software solution can help optimize processes by automating manual tasks, organizing employee records, and building data-driven reports.

Moreover, advanced HR software solutions enable better workforce planning, financial forecasting, and strategic decision-making.

Executive SummaryUpdated on Feb 22, 2026

SmartRecruiters and SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting offer talent acquisition solutions. SmartRecruiters stands out in pricing and support, while SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting is noted for its robust features that justify its higher cost.

Features: SmartRecruiters provides candidate sourcing, job posting flexibility, and ease of use. SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting includes advanced analytics, integration with HR systems, and comprehensive capabilities.

Ease of Deployment and Customer Service: SmartRecruiters is known for straightforward deployment and responsive customer support. SAP SuccessFactors has strong vendor support and thorough training but is more complex.

## Comparison Buyer's Guide

Download the report

Executive SummaryUpdated on Dec 5, 2024

SmartRecruiters and SAP SuccessFactors compete in the HR management software category. SmartRecruiters appears to have an edge in user-friendliness and candidate management capability, whereas SAP SuccessFactors excels in providing comprehensive HR management solutions for larger enterprises.

Features: SmartRecruiters is noted for its simple interface, candidate management features, and diverse sourcing tools, making it ideal for smaller organizations. SAP SuccessFactors offers comprehensive HR management solutions with modularity, talent management, and HR analytics capabilities, suitable for complex large-scale operations.

Room for Improvement: SmartRecruiters faces challenges with global implementation limitations, regional integration issues, and the lack of AI and college recruiting applications. SAP SuccessFactors could improve in providing more agile integration, enhanced analytics, and a better user-friendly experience in reporting and customization.

Ease of Deployment and Customer Service: SmartRecruiters benefits from easy public cloud deployment but encounters issues with technical support responsiveness. SAP SuccessFactors also offers public cloud deployment, with mixed feedback on technical support efficiency. Some users appreciate its responsiveness, while others find it slow and cumbersome.

Pricing and ROI: SmartRecruiters is perceived as expensive but offers a significant ROI, especially for organizations with high recruitment intensity. SAP SuccessFactors, though costly, provides modular pricing flexibility that benefits larger companies, offering a comprehensive feature set that translates into lasting benefits and ROI.

## Executive Summary

SAP Success Factors Recruiting is the heavyweight champion of enterprise talent acquisition—powerful, comprehensive, and demanding. After managing a three-year implementation and operation across our 15,000-employee global organization, I can tell you it's simultaneously one of the most capable and most complex recruiting various competing platforms like Ashby's approach. If you need enterprise-grade functionality and have the resources to manage it properly, Success Factors delivers. If you're looking for simplicity, look elsewhere.

This has been going on now for 8+ weeks, where approximately 30%-40% of our candidates have profiles without resumes because when they try to upload them, the system just spins. This is a known issue and we logged a ticket for this on March 9th, however, we're not closer to seeing this fixed than we were originally. After some back and forth, it's been stated that this is an issue that affects more than just my company as it's something to do with the delivered resume upload/parsing/document management process that SuccessFactors has and something to do with the vendor they use for it (Textkernel). bollarfook 

 

# Best recruiting software for hiring and talent acquisition?

Hi guys. I'm a hiring manager at a fast-growing tech startup (we're scaling from 50 to 200+ employees in the next year), and I'm drowning in resumes and interviews. We're looking to level up our talent acquisition process with a new HR recruiting software, but the options are a bit overwhelming. I would appreciate if you could share what your company uses, and why.

I've done some initial research on top ATS (Applicant Tracking Systems) and hiring tools, but I want real user recommendations from people who've actually used them in high-growth environments.

A bit about our needs: We're hiring for roles across engineering, sales, marketing, and ops. We need a recruiting tool that handles high-volume applicant tracking, automates resume screening, integrates with LinkedIn and other job boards, and maybe even has AI features for candidate matching or interview scheduling.

Budget-wise, we're open to mid-tier options (not the cheapest free tiers, but not enterprise-level pricing either, I guess somewhere between $5k-$20k annually).

# Recruitment software I've looked at so far

Greenhouse: Seems popular for structured hiring processes and reporting. Anyone using it for remote teams?

Lever: Heard it's great for collaborative recruiting and pipeline management. How's the mobile app?

Workable: Affordable and user-friendly, but is it scalable for 100+ hires a year?

BambooHR: More of an all-in-one HR system, but their recruiting module looks good. Worth it if we're already using something else for payroll?

Ashby: Newer player with strong analytics. Any experiences with their AI tools for talent sourcing?

I'm also curious about open-source or lesser-known recruitment platforms like Recruitee, JazzHR, or Zoho Recruit. How do they stack up against the best recruiting software options in terms of features like diversity hiring tools, custom workflows, or integration with tools like Google Workspace or Slack?

Pros/cons, pricing tips, implementation stories, as well as or success stories would be super helpful. If you've switched from one recruiting software to another, what made you jump ship? Thanks in advance for the advice.

P.S. Mods, I hope this post isn't against the rules. I would really appreciate input from people who work in HR or who know what their past or current companies use as recruiting tools. Thank you!

## 2 Answers

Last answered Jan 16, 2026

Chief Executive Officer at Orane Consulting Pvt Ltd

Real User

Top 5 Leaderboard

Jan 16, 2026

There is no complexity in deploying SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting. Over a period of time, we understand the nuances and are comfortable with everything. Employee Central to SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting integration is still a weak area that needs improvement. We are now able to integrate with LLM models outside SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting. With AI, we can provide all those touchpoints as AI integrations in reports and dashboards. Vanilla reports and dashboards are not user-friendly and not beneficial. However, when we integrate with Employee Central and the outside world, integrating these data sets with AI, people are able to realize those values.

### Share this article

After evaluating 14 HR platforms, Rippling is my top pick overall, BambooHR is the most ideal for small teams, Gusto is optimal for new businesses, and ADP Workforce Now is the best fit for midsize firms.

## How does HR software improve your business processes?

Human resources (HR) software systems unify administration, recruitment, payroll, training, employee engagement, performance management, and other essential HR functions.

This provides a secure database of employee data and a centralized view of the company. It also helps HR teams effectively manage each stage of the employee life cycle.

The right HR software solution can help optimize processes by automating manual tasks, organizing employee records, and building data-driven reports.

Moreover, advanced HR software solutions enable better workforce planning, financial forecasting, and strategic decision-making.

## Which HR tools ranked the highest?

I reviewed 13 human resources software and narrowed them down to the best of the best:

## What is SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting?

SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting empowers organizations to secure top talent using data-driven strategies, automation, and engaging candidate experiences. It is designed to streamline recruitment processes, aligning with global growth and transformational goals.

Get the Talent Acquisition Buyer's Guide and find out what your peers are saying about SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting, SmartRecruiters, SAP SuccessFactors Onboarding and more!

## Valuable Features

- "In terms of processes, we are able to provide ROI measurement showing that what used to take 30 days for an open position now takes 50% or 70% of that time with AI features and outside world social media integrations, video integrations, and other tools."
- "SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting is valuable for recruitment; it is web-based, which is not amazing, but it does the work and is handling all our requirements."

## Room for Improvement

- "Employee Central to SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting integration is still a weak area that needs improvement."
- "There are a lot of components that need to be configured, and it requires BTP to integrate to the ECC. SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting is quite complex. It is not straightforward to use."

These insights are based on the in-depth reviews provided by peers to help you make a better buying decision.

Executive SummaryUpdated on Feb 22, 2026

SmartRecruiters and SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting offer talent acquisition solutions. SmartRecruiters stands out in pricing and support, while SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting is noted for its robust features that justify its higher cost.

Features: SmartRecruiters provides candidate sourcing, job posting flexibility, and ease of use. SAP SuccessFactors Recruiting includes advanced analytics, integration with HR systems, and comprehensive capabilities.

Ease of Deployment and Customer Service: SmartRecru

## Featured SAP SuccessFactors Learning reviews

Vice President & Group Head People & Workplace Management at PLDT Enterprise

The GUI of SAP SuccessFactors Learning is still not very good. The drop-downs are too limited. One thing I want to have is an advisory banner with highlighted font that employees can visibly see during login, but support indicated this cannot be done. I have already raised this request to the support team, and they mentioned that the same request has come from other companies.

In the future, I suggest updates primarily on the mobile user experience side, reporting, dashboarding, and workflows. An AI version would definitely help significantly. After evaluating 14 HR platforms, Rippling is my top pick overall, BambooHR is the most ideal for small teams, Gusto is optimal for new businesses, and ADP Workforce Now is the best fit for midsize firms.

## How does HR software improve your business processes?

Human resources (HR) software systems unify administration, recruitment, payroll, training, employee engagement, performance management, and other essential HR functions.

This provides a secure database of employee data and a centralized view of the company. It also helps HR teams effectively manage each stage of the employee life cycle.

The right HR software solution can help optimize processes by automating manual tasks, organizing employee records, and building data-driven reports.

Moreover, advanced HR software solutions enable better workforce planning, financial forecasting, and strategic decision-making.

Best Enterprise LMS Software: 20 Perfect Options 

 

 

 

 

Reports show that the LMS market is expected to grow by almost 250% by 2033, and that’s for a reason. Around 91% of L&D pros say human skills are increasingly important for business growth. And LMSs for enterprises are perceived as the best way to upskill employees.

Businesses often start with their own learning solution, but as the company grows, something bigger, more powerful, and more efficient is needed. In this article, we’ve chosen the 20 best enterprise LMS software options that offer more than simple employee training and can cover most big business needs. Let’s examine them together!

## What is an enterprise LMS, and how should you choose one?

Choosing an LMS is easy when you need to gather your 15 employees together and show them the working rules. Basically, PowerPoint and any screencasting app are a good fit. But as the company grows, it gets harder to train dozens or hundreds or thousands of people.

One day, you’ll need a solution that enables you to author your own courses, make them interactive, and track results — and before you know it, the list of requirements gets extremely long! At that point, you’re looking for a bigger solution: probably an AI-powered, enterprise-level LMS that supports all your HR processes and organizational needs.

So, finding the best enterprise LMS that will cover all big enterprises’ ambitions and needs is not a simple task. For those seeking a quick solution to this challenge, we prepared a comparison chart of the best enterprise LMSs. For more details, click on the LMS or scroll down.

| Enterprise LMS systems | Scalability | Integrations | Extended-enterprise* | Authoring and content | Mobile-friendly |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Absorb LMS | Top enterprise LMS scalability | RESTful API, SSO, HRIS and more | From authoring to selling | Moderate, limited | Native mobile app |
| iSpring LMS | Top enterprise LMS scalability | Albato, RESTful API, SSO, HRIS, CRMs and more | From authoring to selling | Strong (via iSpring Suite) | Native mobile app |
| Cornerstone Learning | Highly scalable | HRIS, SSO, APIs | Strong | Moderate | Native mobile app |

## What is SAP SuccessFactors Learning?
The SAP SuccessFactors Learning solution helps prepare people for the future with innovative capabilities to drive skills management, learning, and development. With a unified corporate learning management system (LMS), you can boost employee skills while helping ensure compliance. SAP SuccessFactors Learning supports employee training and reduces compliance risk with a modern learning experience.

## What is SAP SuccessFactors Learning?

SAP SuccessFactors Learning empowers organizations with AI-driven tools for personalized learning and skills development, aligning corporate objectives with individual employee growth paths.

Get the SAP SuccessFactors Learning Buyer's Guide and find out what your peers are saying about SAP SuccessFactors Learning, Cornerstone Learn, Moodle and more!

SAP SuccessFactors Learning is the #1 ranked solution in top Learning Management Systems. PeerSpot users give SAP SuccessFactors Learning an average rating of 8.0 out of 10. ## How does HR software improve your business processes?

Human resources (HR) software systems unify administration, recruitment, payroll, training, employee engagement, performance management, and other essential HR functions.

This provides a secure database of employee data and a centralized view of the company. It also helps HR teams effectively manage each stage of the employee life cycle.

The right HR software solution can help optimize processes by automating manual tasks, organizing employee records, and building data-driven reports.

Hi Experts. Would appreciate some help on this issue.

Goals cannot be viewed on mobile when accessed via Navigation Bar > Profile > Performance and Goals (but is visible via the same path on web)

The goals however can be viewed on mobile via Navigation Bar > Goals.

## Comparison Buyer's Guide

Download the report

Executive SummaryUpdated on Feb 22, 2026

SAP SuccessFactors and SAP SuccessFactors Performance & Goals compete in the HR management category. SAP SuccessFactors generally has the edge with broader HR capabilities, while Performance & Goals is superior in targeted performance tracking.

Features: SAP SuccessFactors includes onboarding, employee central management, and payroll integration. Performance & Goals provides goal setting, continuous performance management, and comprehensive review cycles.

Ease of Deployment and Customer Service: SAP SuccessFactors offers wide integration options for a smooth transition, while Performance & Goals simplifies implementation with a focus on performance processes. Both provide responsive customer service, with Performance & Goals potentially offering quicker support due to its focused scope.

Pricing and ROI: SAP SuccessFactors involves a higher initial setup cost, yielding significant ROI by improving workforce efficiency. Performance & Goals has a lower initial cost, delivering quicker ROI for companies focused on performance and goal management.

# Sales Compensation Xactly Incent vs SAP Success Factors Incentive Management

Compare Xactly Incent and SAP Success Factors Incentive Management using real user data focused on features, satisfaction, business value, and the vendor relationship.

## What is Sales Compensation Software?

Sales Compensation Software also referred to as Sales Incentive Compensation Management (ICM) allows the creation, management, and tracking of compensation, commissions and incentive plans for an organizations sales teams. Commission structures can often be complicated and convoluted but the software can display this in a simplified, transparent way as well as provide answers to common questions from salespeople on their commissions.

## Common Features

Incentive Plan Designer | Regulatory Compliance and Audit | Data Integration | Reporting and Analytics | Commissions Management | Pre-Built Incentive Plans | Incentive Dashboards | Collaboration | Multi Currency | Adjustments & Clawbacks | AI Coach | Earnings Simulator

# 5 Reasons Why You Should Not Manage Compensation in SAP SuccessFactors

Senem Birim

||

Published:

August 29, 2025

Senem Birim

||

Published:

August 29, 2025

About Author

Summarize with AI

Picture this: Your company already runs SAP SuccessFactors (SF) for HR. When it's time to set up compensation management, the obvious choice seems clear - "Why not just handle it all in one place?"

This makes sense on the surface. One platform should mean less complexity and fewer tools to manage.

However, here's what most HR teams discover after embarking on this path: compensation is unlike other HR processes. It's highly dynamic, needs constant adjustments, and requires tools that can adapt quickly to changing business needs.SAP SuccessFactors wasn't purpose-built for the nuanced world of compensation planning.

Let's explore five reasons why trying to force your comp processes into SAP SF often creates more headaches than solutions.

## Common Hesitations about Switching from SAP SuccessFactors to Compensation Platforms

Before diving into the specific problems, let's acknowledge the elephant in the room. Many HR leaders hesitate to move away from SAP SuccessFactors compensation for understandable reasons.

"We want to keep everything on one platform," they say. This feels like the safe, integrated choice.

But here's what HR leaders are realizing: true integration isn't just about system uniformity — it's about experience, agility, and impact.

A specialized compensation solution can still integrate tightly with SAP while delivering far more configurability and insight.

## Reason 1: Clunky interface drives managers back to Excel

The problem: SAP SuccessFactors' compensation module feels clunky and unintuitive. One Reddit user described it as "a patchwork of independently developed modules" that's "surprisingly slow and buggy."

Source

Source

What it means

- Planning cycles slow down. Managers make mistakes, miss deadlines, or refuse to engage. HR spends time troubleshooting instead of making strategic decisions.
- Managers often avoid the complex interface and revert to using Excel spreadsheets. You end up paying for a digital solution while people use manual workarounds.

The alternative

- When managers can navigate easily, the enti
```

## What is SAP SuccessFactors?

SAP SuccessFactors is an AI-powered, cloud-based HR suite supporting over 100 countries, providing real-time insights and integrated solutions across core HR, payroll, talent, learning, analytics, and employee experience.

Get the SAP SuccessFactors Buyer's Guide and find out what your peers are saying about SAP SuccessFactors, Workday, Oracle HCM Cloud and more!

## Featured SAP SuccessFactors reviews

SS

Assistant Manager at Kashiv Biosciences

SAP SuccessFactors has a low error rate. We had many ad hoc reports that we needed to generate, and it was very easy to do so in SAP SuccessFactors. We also created many in-house reports according to our specific requirements with the help of this tool, which was a really big game changer for us. We did not depend on advanced Excel in those cases. We generated a lot of detailed reports whenever we needed them during emergency cases or board meetings. A lot of usefulness and time were saved in those cases. I will also mention that we conducted a comparative study for some recruitment cases. We had a recruitment model where we were looking for a very niche profile. Since the job profile was really different and rare, we had to depend on analytics to understand and shortlist from a large pool of candidates that we already had in our database. Analytics was really helpful in this situation.

Succession Planning Software
# Succession Planning SoftwareReviews and Ratings
Download PDF
## What is Succession Planning Software?
Succession planning is a tool used by organizations to identify and develop new leaders within a company to replace old leaders when they leave, retire, or are promoted. It is the means of preserving a company's future and its associated stakeholders. Managers, Senior Management, HR professionals and Talent Acquisition teamsuse this tool to map out career paths, identifying skills gaps, and prepare employees for future roles to ensure a smooth transition and continuity in key positions. It includes features like talent pools, development plans, and analytics to assess and track the readiness of potential successors.

## What is SAP SuccessFactors?

SAP SuccessFactors is an AI-powered, cloud-based HR suite supporting over 100 countries, providing real-time insights and integrated solutions across core HR, payroll, talent, learning, analytics, and employee experience.

Get the SAP SuccessFactors Buyer's Guide and find out what your peers are saying about SAP SuccessFactors, Workday, Oracle HCM Cloud and more!

## Featured SAP SuccessFactors reviews

SS

Assistant Manager at Kashiv Biosciences

SAP SuccessFactors has a low error rate. We had many ad hoc reports that we needed to generate, and it was very easy to do so in SAP SuccessFactors. We also created many in-house reports according to our specific requirements with the help of this tool, which was a really big game changer for us. We did not depend on advanced Excel in those cases. We generated a lot of detailed reports whenever we needed them during emergency cases or board meetings. A lot of usefulness and time were saved in those cases. I will also mention that we conducted a comparative study for some recruitment cases. We had a recruitment model where we were looking for a very niche profile. Since the job profile was really different and rare, we had to depend on analytics to understand and shortlist from a large pool of candidates that we already had in our database. Analytics was really helpful in this situation.

Succession Planning Software
# Succession Planning SoftwareReviews and Ratings
Download PDF
## What is Succession Planning Software?
Succession planning is a tool used by organizations to identify and develop new leaders within a company to replace old leaders when they leave, retire, or are promoted. It is the means of preserving a company's future and its associated stakeholders. Managers, Senior Management, HR professionals and Talent Acquisition teamsuse this tool to map out career paths, identifying skills gaps, and prepare employees for future roles to ensure a smooth transition and continuity in key positions. It includes features like talent pools, development plans, and analytics to assess and track the readiness of potential successors.

# SAP Fell 13% in the Last 30 Days. Here’s How Much the Stock Could Rise in 2026

Nikko Henson• 4 minute read

Reviewed by: Thomas Richmond

Last updated Feb 16, 2026

 

 

 

### Key Stats for SAP SE Stock

- Last 30-Day Performance: -13%
- 52-Week Range: $169 to $289
- Valuation Model Target Price: $334
- Implied Upside: 24%

Value your favorite stocks like SAP SE with 5 years of analysts’ forecasts using TIKR’s new Valuation Model (It’s free) >>>

## What Happened?

SAP SE stock fell about 13% in the last 30 days, recently trading near $205 per share as investors rotated out of enterprise software names and compressed valuation multiples across large-cap SaaS stocks.

The stock declined specifically because current cloud backlog growth slowed to 25% to EUR 21 billion, which came in below investor expectations, even though total cloud backlog rose 30% to EUR 77 billion. Markets focused on the deceleration in near-term backlog momentum rather than the record long-term pipeline, triggering multiple compression despite otherwise strong operating results.

In the last 30 days, SAP reported full-year cloud revenue growth of 26%, marking continued strength in its subscription transition. Q4 was the company’s best bookings quarter of the year, with large cloud deals above EUR 5 million representing a record 71% of cloud order entry. CEO Christian Klein said, “we overachieved and beat our outlook for operating profit and cash flow,” as non-IFRS operating profit reached EUR 10.4 billion and free cash flow totaled EUR 8.2 billion.

Management also guided for approximately EUR 10 billion in free cash flow in 2026 and announced a new EUR 10 billion share repurchase program. The recent decline appears driven by sentiment and short-term backlog optics rather than weakening fundamentals or demand.

SAP SE Guided Valuation Model

See analysts’ growth forecasts and price targets for SAP SE (It’s free) >>>

## Is SAP SE Undervalued?

Under valuation assumptions, the stock is modeled using:

- Revenue Growth (CAGR): 10.6%
- Operating Margins: 30.6%
- Exit P/E Multiple: 28x

Revenue growth is increasingly supported by S/4HANA migrations and RISE with SAP adoption as enterprises modernize core ERP systems and move toward multi-year subscription contracts.

Cloud revenue grew 26% last year and total cloud backlog reached EUR 77 billion, providing strong multi-year visibility into recurring revenue streams.

# SAP stock forecast: Third-party price targets

SAP is a Germany-listed enterprise software company providing business applications and cloud services to organisations worldwide, with its shares traded across multiple European and international markets. Explore third-party SAP price targets and technical analysis.

SAPd -0.94%

By Dan Mitchell 14:49 (UTC), 10 February 2026

Photo: Shutterstock.com

SAP SE (SAP) is trading around €168.50 in intraday European dealing at 4:10pm (UTC) on 5 February 2026, within a session range of approximately €160.05–€173.50 and broadly in line with recent moves in wider European equities. Past performance is not a reliable indicator of future results.

The move comes amid continued focus on SAP’s recently reported Q4 and full-year 2025 results, in which the company highlighted double-digit total revenue growth and a strong expansion in cloud backlog, underlining an ongoing shift toward cloud and software-as-a-service contracts (SAP, 29 January 2026). This price action has also tracked broader Euro Area equity trading, where the Euro Stoxx 50 index was little changed on 5 February 2026, and SAP shares on the cash market were reported up around 3% on the day, contributing to large-cap technology and industrials performance across the region (Trading Economics, 5 February 2026).

## SAP stock forecast 2026–2030: Third-party price targets

As of 5 February 2026, third-party SAP stock predictions summarise six third-party one-year target markers and the assumptions cited by each source.

### J.P. Morgan (target cut after earnings)

J.P. Morgan lowered its SAP stock forecast from €290 to €260 on 30 January 2026, while maintaining an Overweight rating. The broker cites softer-than-expected growth in SAP’s current cloud backlog and a general weakening in software-sector sentiment as reasons for adjusting valuation multiples after the Q4 2025 release (MarketScreener, 30 January 2026).

### Berenberg (revised downside and valuation)

Finimize notes that Berenberg cut its SAP target from €280 to €250, retaining a Buy recommendation. The bank explains the reduction by pointing to a lower valuation multiple amid weaker market sentiment and trimmed revenue projections, after the stock fell sharply on the Xetra market in late January (Finimize, 2 February 2026).

SAP Quarterly Statement Q4 2025 Accessibility Statement Skip Navigation

- SAP meets revenue and exceeds non-IFRS operating profit and free cash flow outlook for FY2025
- Total cloud backlog up 22% and up 30% at constant currencies
- Current cloud backlog up 16% and up 25% at constant currencies

- Cloud ERP Suite revenue up 28% and up 32% at constant currencies in FY2025
- Total revenue up 8% and up 11% at constant currencies in FY2025
- IFRS operating profit up 111%, non-IFRS operating profit up 28% and up 31% at constant currencies in FY2025
- SAP announces a new, two-year share repurchase program with a volume of up to €10 billion

WALLDORF, Germany, Jan. 29, 2026 /PRNewswire/ -- SAP SE (NYSE: SAP) announced today its financial results for the fourth quarter and fiscal year ended December 31, 2025.

Christian Klein, CEO:Q4 was a strong cloud quarter, with bookings resulting in 30% Total Cloud Backlog growth to a record 77 billion Euros. The significant Current Cloud Backlog growth in Q4 has laid a strong foundation for accelerating Total Revenue growth through 2027. SAP Business AI has become a main driver for growth as it was included in two thirds of our Q4 cloud order entry, combined with strong AI adoption across the ERP Suite.

Dominik Asam, CFO:We closed 2025 on a high note, delivering strong operating profit and free cash flow ahead of our expectations. This performance reflects focused execution, financial discipline, and the continued trust our customers place in us as the North Star for their digital transformation. As evidenced by continued strong growth well ahead of the market in SaaS and PaaS, and our ability to bring such growth down to the bottom line and Free Cash Flow, we are confident that our strategy and operational discipline will continue to drive long-term value creation.

Financial Performance

Group results at a glance – Fourth quarter 2025
